--Students table
CREATE TABLE Students
(
  Epoka_ID CHAR(8) NOT NULL,
  Personal_ID CHAR(10) NOT NULL,
  Name VARCHAR(12) NOT NULL,
  Surname VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
  Birthday DATE NOT NULL,
  Gender VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
  Birth_Place VARCHAR(12) NOT NULL,
  Blood_Type VARCHAR(3),
  Martial_Status BOOLEAN NOT NULL,
  Citizenship VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
  Passaport_No VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
  Primary_email VARCHAR(320) NOT NULL,
  Secondary_email VARCHAR(320) NOT NULL,
  Exam_ID CHAR(5) NOT NULL,
  Status BOOLEAN NOT NULL,
  CGPA FLOAT NOT NULL CHECK (CGPA >= 0),
  Enrollment_Date DATE NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (Epoka_ID)
);

--Lecturer table
CREATE TABLE Lecturer
(
  Lecturer_ID CHAR(10) NOT NULL,
  Name VARCHAR(30) NOT NULL,
  office VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
  email VARCHAR(320) NOT NULL,
  office_phone CHAR(15) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (Lecturer_ID)
);

--Lecturer_info table
CREATE TABLE Lecturer_info
(
  Type VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
  info VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
  Lecturer_ID CHAR(10) NOT NULL,
  FOREIGN KEY (Lecturer_ID) REFERENCES Lecturer(Lecturer_ID) ON UPDATE CASCADE ON DELETE CASCADE
);

--Student_Documents table
CREATE TABLE Student_Documents
(
  Type VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
  Info VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
  Epoka_ID CHAR(8) NOT NULL,
  FOREIGN KEY (Epoka_ID) REFERENCES Students(Epoka_ID) ON UPDATE CASCADE ON DELETE CASCADE
);

--Faculty table
CREATE TABLE Faculty
(
  Faculty_name INT NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (Faculty_name)
);

-- Updated Departament table
CREATE TABLE Departament
(
  Departament_name INT NOT NULL,
  Faculty_name INT NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (Departament_name),
  FOREIGN KEY (Faculty_name) REFERENCES Faculty(Faculty_name) ON UPDATE CASCADE ON DELETE SET NULL
);

-- Updated Study_Programs table
CREATE TABLE Study_Programs
(
  Study_Program_ID CHAR(5) NOT NULL,
  Name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
  Type VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
  Departament_name INT NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (Study_Program_ID),
  FOREIGN KEY (Departament_name) REFERENCES Departament(Departament_name) ON UPDATE CASCADE ON DELETE SET NULL
);

--Courses table
CREATE TABLE Courses
(
  Course_ID CHAR(10) NOT NULL,
  Code VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
  Course_type CHAR(1) NOT NULL,
  Theory INT NOT NULL CHECK (Theory >= 0),
  Practice INT NOT NULL CHECK (Practice >= 0),
  Lab INT CHECK (Lab >= 0),
  Credits INT NOT NULL CHECK (Credits > 0),
  Ects INT NOT NULL CHECK (Ects > 0),
  Total_Hours INT NOT NULL CHECK (Total_Hours >0),
  Study_Program_ID CHAR(5) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (Course_ID),
  FOREIGN KEY (Study_Program_ID) REFERENCES Study_Programs(Study_Program_ID) ON UPDATE CASCADE ON DELETE SET NULL
);

--Course_completion table
CREATE TABLE Course_completion
(
  Attendence FLOAT NOT NULL CHECK (Attendence >= 0 AND Attendence <= 100),
  Course_Completion FLOAT NOT NULL CHECK (Course_Completion >= 0 AND Course_Completion <= 100),
  Overall_grade FLOAT NOT NULL CHECK (Overall_grade >= 0),
  Epoka_ID CHAR(8) NOT NULL,
  Course_ID CHAR(10) NOT NULL,
  FOREIGN KEY (Epoka_ID) REFERENCES Students(Epoka_ID) ON UPDATE CASCADE ON DELETE SET NULL,
  FOREIGN KEY (Course_ID) REFERENCES Courses(Course_ID) ON UPDATE CASCADE ON DELETE SET NULL
);

--Assignments table
CREATE TABLE Assignments
(
  Name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
  Type VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
  Weight FLOAT NOT NULL CHECK (Weight >= 0 AND Weight <= 100),
  Class_Average FLOAT NOT NULL CHECK (Class_Average >= 0 AND Class_Average <= 100),
  assignment_ID INT NOT NULL,
  Course_ID CHAR(10) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (assignment_ID),
  FOREIGN KEY (Course_ID) REFERENCES Courses(Course_ID) ON UPDATE CASCADE ON DELETE SET NULL
);

--Gives table
CREATE TABLE Gives
(
  Course_ID CHAR(10) NOT NULL,
  Lecturer_ID CHAR(10) NOT NULL,
  FOREIGN KEY (Course_ID) REFERENCES Courses(Course_ID) ON UPDATE CASCADE ON DELETE SET NULL,
  FOREIGN KEY (Lecturer_ID) REFERENCES Lecturer(Lecturer_ID) ON UPDATE CASCADE ON DELETE SET NULL
);

--Course_info table
CREATE TABLE Course_info
(
  Type VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
  info VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
  Course_ID CHAR(10) NOT NULL,
  FOREIGN KEY (Course_ID) REFERENCES Courses(Course_ID) ON UPDATE CASCADE ON DELETE CASCADE
);

--Attendence table
CREATE TABLE Attendence
(
  Week VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
  Type VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
  Hours_Attended VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
  Date DATE NOT NULL,
  Topic VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
  Epoka_ID CHAR(8) NOT NULL,
  Course_ID CHAR(10) NOT NULL,
  FOREIGN KEY (Epoka_ID) REFERENCES Students(Epoka_ID) ON UPDATE CASCADE ON DELETE SET NULL,
  FOREIGN KEY (Course_ID) REFERENCES Courses(Course_ID) ON UPDATE CASCADE ON DELETE SET NULL
);

--Groups table
CREATE TABLE Groups
(
  Group_ID VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
  number_of_students INT NOT NULL CHECK (number_of_students > 0),
  class_average FLOAT NOT NULL CHECK (class_average >= 0 AND class_average <= 100),
  Course_ID CHAR(10) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (Group_ID),
  FOREIGN KEY (Course_ID) REFERENCES Courses(Course_ID) ON UPDATE CASCADE ON DELETE SET NULL
);

--Interim_Grades table
CREATE TABLE Interim_Grades
(
  grade INT NOT NULL CHECK (grade >= 0 AND grade <= 100),
  Epoka_ID CHAR(8) NOT NULL,
  assignment_ID INT NOT NULL,
  FOREIGN KEY (Epoka_ID) REFERENCES Students(Epoka_ID) ON UPDATE CASCADE ON DELETE SET NULL,
  FOREIGN KEY (assignment_ID) REFERENCES Assignments(assignment_ID) ON UPDATE CASCADE ON DELETE SET NULL
);

--Student_is_in_group table
CREATE TABLE Student_is_in_group
(
  Epoka_ID CHAR(8) NOT NULL,
  Group_ID VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
  FOREIGN KEY (Epoka_ID) REFERENCES Students(Epoka_ID) ON UPDATE CASCADE ON DELETE SET NULL,
  FOREIGN KEY (Group_ID) REFERENCES Groups(Group_ID) ON UPDATE CASCADE ON DELETE SET NULL
);

--triggers for Overall Grade

CREATE TRIGGER change_overallGrade
AFTER INSERT ON Interim_Grades
FOR EACH ROW
BEGIN
    UPDATE Course_completion
    SET Overall_grade = (
        SELECT SUM(grade * weight / 100)
        FROM Interim_Grades
        JOin Assignments on Interim_Grades.assignment_ID = Assignments.assignment_ID
        WHERE Interim_Grades.Epoka_ID = NEW.Epoka_ID
    )
    WHERE Course_completion.Epoka_ID = NEW.Epoka_ID;
END;

CREATE TRIGGER change_overallGrade2
AFTER UPDATE ON Interim_Grades
FOR EACH ROW
BEGIN
    UPDATE Course_completion
    SET Overall_grade = (
        SELECT SUM(grade * weight / 100)
        FROM Interim_Grades
        JOin Assignments on Interim_Grades.assignment_ID = Assignments.assignment_ID
        WHERE Interim_Grades.Epoka_ID = NEW.Epoka_ID
    )
    WHERE Course_completion.Epoka_ID = NEW.Epoka_ID;
END;
